| <span data-ttu-id="d327e-708">Voce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d327e-708">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d327e-709">Valore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d327e-709">Value</span></span> |

## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="d327e-1063">Attributi di Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d327e-1063">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d327e-1064">Questa classe contiene gli attributi seguenti per Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d327e-1064">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
